    ```shell
    # describe æ•°æ®åº“è¡¨å;
    mysql> describe network3;

    # ==========================================================================

    # å‘æ•°æ®è¡¨ä¸­æ·»åŠ æ•°æ®
    # insert into æ•°æ®åº“è¡¨å values(valueå€¼1,valueå€¼2,.......);
    # insert into æ•°æ®åº“è¡¨å (åˆ—å1,åˆ—å2,...ï¼‰ values(valueå€¼1,valueå€¼2,...);
    mysql> insert into network3 values("3114006441","xpleaf","male",35,"QingYuan");
    mysql> insert into network3 values("3114006442","Pei","male",41,"PuNing");
    mysql> insert into network3 values("3114006443","Jim","male",38,"JiangMen");
    mysql> insert into network3 values("3114006440","Xuan","male",36,"ShanWei");
    mysql> insert into network3 values("3114006440","Ting","female",30,"ChaoShan");
    mysql> insert into network3 values("3114006336","Ting","female",30,"ChaoShan");

    # ==========================================================================

    # æŸ¥è¯¢æ•°æ®åº“è¡¨ä¸­çš„æ•°æ®
    # select åˆ—åç§° from æ•°æ®åº“è¡¨å [æŸ¥è¯¢æ¡ä»¶];
    mysql> select * from network3;
    mysql> select id,name from network3;
    mysql> select * from network3 where name='xpleaf';
    mysql> select * from network3 where sex="male";
    mysql> select * from network3 where sex="female";
    mysql> select * from network3 where sex="male" and address="QingYuan";
    mysql> select * from network3 where age < 40 and age > 31;
    mysql> select * from network3 where name like "%leaf";
    mysql> select * from network3 where name like "%i";
    mysql> select * from network3 where name like "%i%";
    mysql> select * from network3 where name like "i";
    mysql> select * from network3 where name like "i%";
    mysql> select * from network3 where name like "%i%";
    mysql> select * from network3;

    # ==========================================================================

    # ä¿®æ”¹æ•°æ®åº“è¡¨ä¸­çš„æ•°æ®
    # update æ•°æ®åº“åˆ—å set åˆ—å¤Ÿ=æ–°value where æ›´æ–°æ¡ä»¶;
    mysql> update network3 set address="YuanTan" where name="xpleaf";
    mysql> select * from network3;

    mysql> update network3 set name="Hui" where id="3114006336";
    mysql> select * from network3;

    # è¿™æ˜¯æˆ‘å†™é”™çš„
    mysql> update network3 set age=age+=1;
    mysql> select * from network3;

    mysql> update network3 set age=age+1;
    mysql> select * from network3;

    mysql> delete from network3 where name="Pei";
    mysql> select * from network3;

    # ==========================================================================

    # ä¿®æ”¹æ•°æ®åº“è¡¨çš„ã€ç»“æ„ã€‘
    # alter table æ•°æ®åº“è¡¨å change åˆ—åç§° æ–°æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ [å…¶å®ƒ];

    # å…ˆ çœ‹ä¸€ä¸‹æ•°æ®è¡¨çš„è¯¦ç»†ä¿¡æ¯
    mysql> describe network3;

    #ä¿®æ”¹åˆ—
    mysql> alter table network3 change address addr char(30) not null;
    mysql> alter table network3 change name name char(20) not null;
    mysql> alter table network3 change sex Sex char(10) not null;
    mysql> describe network3;

    # åˆ é™¤åˆ—
    mysql> alter table network3 drop addr;
    mysql> describe network3;
    # çœ‹å®Œè¡¨ç»“æ„ï¼Œå†çœ‹ä¸€ä¸‹æ ‡çš„æ•°æ®æ˜¯ä¸æ˜¯ä¹Ÿè¢«åˆ æ‰äº†
    mysql> select * from network3;

    # é‡å‘½åæ•°æ®åº“è¡¨
    mysql> alter table network3 rename New_network3;
    mysql> show tables;

    # åˆ é™¤æ•°æ®åº“è¡¨
    mysql> drop table New_network3;
    mysql> show tables

    # ==========================================================================
    
    # åˆ é™¤æ•°æ®åº“
    # å…ˆçœ‹ä¸€ä¸‹æ‰€æœ‰çš„æ•°æ®åº“
    mysql> show databases;

    # åˆ é™¤ï¼Œæˆ‘å†™é”™äº†
    mysql> drop students_info;

    # æ­£ç¡®çš„åˆ é™¤
    mysql> drop database students_info;
    mysql> show databases;

    # é€€å‡º mysql
    mysql> quit    
    ```

### 31æ—¥
- æŸ¥æ‰¾å‘½ä»¤çš„ä½ç½® `where`
    ```bash
    where git
    /usr/bin/git
    ```
- æˆ‘çš„ Mac è‡ªå¸¦çš„ git
    ```shell
    git --version
    git version 2.24.3 (Apple Git-128)
    ```
- [ä¼˜é›…çš„å¸è½½Macé»˜è®¤çš„Xcodeé™„å¸¦çš„git](https://www.w3cschool.cn/cuhkj/cuhkj-1k5l265q.html) æ€è·¯æ˜¯æ›´æ”¹ ç¯å¢ƒå˜é‡çš„æŒ‡å‘

- date æ ¼å¼æ ‡å‡† [å‘ç°æ¥æº](https://git-scm.com/docs/git-log#Documentation/git-log.txt-emadem)
    - %cD : committer date, RFC2822 style
        - `Fri, 3 Jul 2020 10:57:24 +0800`
    - %cr : committer date, relative
        - `4 weeks ago`
    - %ct : committer date, UNIX timestamp
        - `1593745044`
    - %ci : committer date, ISO 8601-like format
        - `2020-07-03 10:57:24 +0800`
    - %cI : committer date, strict ISO 8601 format
        - `2020-07-03T10:57:24+08:00`
    - %cs : committer date, short format (YYYY-MM-DD)

- [Gitå…¨å±€é…ç½®å’Œå•ä¸ªä»“åº“çš„ç”¨æˆ·åé‚®ç®±é…ç½®](https://blog.csdn.net/dcj3sjt126com/article/details/84739380)
- git æ›´æ”¹å·²ç»æäº¤çš„è®°å½•ä¸­çš„ ç”¨æˆ·åå’Œ é‚®ç®±
    
    ```shell script
    # å…‹éš†
    git clone --bare https://github.com/user/repo.git
  
    # è¿›å…¥ç›®å½•
    cd repo.git
    
    # æ‰§è¡Œè¿™ä¸€æ®µ
    # OLD_EMAIL æ¢æˆä½ è¦è¢«æ›¿æ¢çš„é‚®ç®±
    # CORRECT_NAME æ¢æˆä½ è¦æ›¿æ¢æˆçš„åå­—
    # CORRECT_EMAIL æ¢æˆä½ è¦æ›¿æ¢æˆçš„é‚®ç®±
    git filter-branch --env-filter '
       
    OLD_EMAIL="xxxx@old.com"
    CORRECT_NAME="username"
    CORRECT_EMAIL="yyyy@new.com"
    
    if [ "$GIT_COMMITTER_EMAIL" = "$OLD_EMAIL" ]
    then
    export GIT_COMMITTER_NAME="$CORRECT_NAME"
    export GIT_COMMITTER_EMAIL="$CORRECT_EMAIL"
    fi
    if [ "$GIT_AUTHOR_EMAIL" = "$OLD_EMAIL" ]
    then
    export GIT_AUTHOR_NAME="$CORRECT_NAME"
    export GIT_AUTHOR_EMAIL="$CORRECT_EMAIL"
    fi
    ' --tag-name-filter cat -- --branches --tags
       
    # æ¨é€
    git push --force --tags origin 'refs/heads/*'
    
    # åˆ é™¤è¿™ä¸ªä¸´æ—¶åº“
    cd ../
    rm -rf repo.git
    ```

### 21æ—¥

### 29æ—¥

1. é‡åˆ°ä¸€ä¸ªé—®é¢˜ï¼š

    ```javascript
    function F() {}
    function O() {}

    O.prototype = new F();
    var obj = new O();

    console.log(obj instanceof O); // true
    console.log(obj instanceof F); // true
    console.log(obj.__proto__ === O.prototype); // true
    console.log(obj.__proto__.__proto__ === F.prototype); // true

    // è¿™ä¸ªæˆ‘æ‡‚ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯ç¨å¾®è°ƒæ•´äº†ä¸€ä¸‹ä»£ç é¡ºåºï¼Œä¸ºå•¥è¾“å‡ºå…¨æ˜¯ false
    // prototype çš„æ”¹å†™ä¸æ˜¯ä¼šåº”ç”¨åˆ°æ‰€æœ‰çš„å®ä¾‹å—ï¼Ÿï¼Œä¸ºä»€ä¹ˆè¾“å‡ºç»“æœä¼šå˜æˆ false

    function F() {}
    function O() {}

    var obj = new O();
    O.prototype = new F();

    console.log(obj instanceof O); // false
    console.log(obj instanceof F); // false
    console.log(obj.__proto__ === O.prototype); // false
    console.log(obj.__proto__.__proto__ === F.prototype); // false
    ```

### 26æ—¥

1. ```Promise``` å¯¹è±¡

        - ```fulfilled``` - å·²æˆåŠŸï¼Œåœ¨å¼‚æ­¥æ“ä½œæˆåŠŸæ—¶è°ƒç”¨ï¼Œå¹¶å°†ç»“æœä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ä¼ é€’å‡ºå»ã€‚
        - ```rejected``` - å·²å¤±è´¥ã€‚åœ¨å¼‚æ­¥æ“ä½œå¤±è´¥æ—¶è°ƒç”¨ï¼Œå¹¶å°†æŠ¥å‡ºçš„é”™è¯¯ä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ä¼ é€’å‡ºå»ã€‚

        > ä»åŸºæœ¬ç”¨æ³•çš„ä¾‹å­ä¸­æˆ‘ä»¬çœ‹åˆ°Promiseæ„é€ å‡½æ•°çš„å‚æ•°æ˜¯ ```resolve``` å’Œ ```reject``` ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸æ˜¯ä¸‰ç§çŠ¶æ€ä¸­çš„ ```fulfilled``` å’Œ ```rejected``` ï¼ŒåŸå› å°±æ˜¯ï¼š ```resolved``` è¡¨ç¤ºçš„æ˜¯å·²ç»“æŸï¼ˆå·²å®šå‹ï¼‰ï¼Œå®ƒåŒ…å« ```fullfilled``` å’Œ ```rejected``` ä¸¤ç§çŠ¶æ€ï¼Œä½†ä½¿ç”¨ä¸­ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬é»˜è®¤çš„å°† ```resolved``` å½“åš ```fulfilled``` ï¼ˆæˆåŠŸï¼‰ä½¿ç”¨ã€‚
    - ```Promise``` å¯¹è±¡çš„çŠ¶æ€æ”¹å˜ï¼Œåªæœ‰ä¸¤ç§å¯èƒ½ï¼šä» ```pending``` å˜ä¸º ```fulfilled``` å’Œä» ```pending``` å˜ä¸º ```rejected``` ã€‚
    - åŸºæœ¬ ```API``` 
        1. ```.then()``` 
            > è¯­æ³• ```Promise.prototype.then( onFulfilled, onRejected )```
        2. ```.catch()``` ï¼ŒæŠ›å‡ºå¼‚å¸¸
            > è¯­æ³• ```Promise.prototype.catch( onRejected )```

            ```javascript
            var promise = new Promise(function(resolve, reject){
                // some code 
            })

            promise.then(function(data) {
                console.log('success');
            }, function(error) {
                console.log('error', error);
            });

            // ç­‰ä»·äº
            promise.then(function(data){
                console.log('success');
            }).catch(function(error) {
                console.log('error', error);
            });
            ```
        3. ```.all()``` - ```Promise``` ä¸­çš„â€œ**é€»è¾‘ä¸**â€ï¼ŒåŒæ—¶å¼€å§‹ï¼Œå¹¶è¡Œæ‰§è¡Œ
            > è¯­æ³• ```promise.all( iterable )```

            ```javascript
            var p = Promise.all([p1, p2, p3]);
            ```
            - æ¥æ”¶ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ï¼ˆæˆ–å…·æœ‰ ```Iterator``` æ¥å£ï¼‰ä½œå‚æ•°
            -  ```p1ã€p2ã€p3``` å‡ä¸º ```promise``` å®ä¾‹ï¼Œå¦‚æœä¸æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ª ```promise``` ï¼Œè¯¥é¡¹ä¼šè¢«ç”¨ ```Promise.resolve``` è½¬æ¢ä¸ºä¸€ä¸ª ```promise```
            - å½“ ```p1, p2, p3``` çŠ¶æ€éƒ½å˜ä¸º ```fulfilled``` ï¼Œ ```p``` çš„çŠ¶æ€æ‰ä¼šå˜ä¸º ```fulfilled``` ï¼Œå¹¶å°†ä¸‰ä¸ª ```promise``` è¿”å›çš„ç»“æœï¼ŒæŒ‰å‚æ•°çš„é¡ºåºï¼ˆè€Œä¸æ˜¯ ```resolved``` çš„é¡ºåºï¼‰å­˜å…¥æ•°ç»„ï¼Œä¼ ç»™ ```p``` çš„å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°

            ```javascript
            var p1 = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                setTimeout(resolve, 3000, "first");
            });
            var p2 = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                resolve("second");
            });
            var p3 = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                setTimeout(resolve, 1000, "third");
            });

            Promise.all([p1, p2, p3]).then(function(values) {
                console.log(values);
            });
            
            // çº¦3ç§’å è¾“å‡º
            // ["first", "second", "third"]
            ```
            - å½“ ```p1, p2, p3``` å…¶ä¸­ä¹‹ä¸€çŠ¶æ€å˜ä¸º ```rejected``` ï¼Œ ```p``` çš„çŠ¶æ€ä¹Ÿä¼šå˜ä¸º ```rejected``` ï¼Œå¹¶æŠŠç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªè¢« ```reject``` çš„ promise çš„è¿”å›å€¼ï¼Œç«‹å³è§¦å‘å¹¶ä¼ ç»™ ```p``` çš„å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°
       
            ```javascript
            // å°†ä¸Šä¾‹ä¸­çš„p2é€‚å½“ä¿®æ”¹å¦‚ä¸‹
            var p2 = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                resolve(x);
            });
            ```
            
            - è¿™æ—¶ï¼Œp2ä¼šæŠ›å‡ºé”™è¯¯ï¼Œç«‹å³ä¼ ç»™Promise.all()ï¼Œç»“æŸæ‰§è¡Œã€‚

        4. ```.race()``` - ç«é€Ÿæ‰§è¡Œï¼Œ ```Promise``` ä¸­â€œ**é€»è¾‘æˆ–**â€ï¼Œå…ˆç»“æŸçš„ä¼ å€¼ç»™ ```then```
            > è¯­æ³•ï¼š ```Promise.race( iterable )```
            - ```Promise.race``` æ–¹æ³•åŒæ ·æ¥å—ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ï¼ˆæˆ–å…·æœ‰Iteratoræ¥å£ï¼‰ä½œå‚æ•°
            - å½“ ```p1, p2, p3``` ä¸­æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªå®ä¾‹çš„çŠ¶æ€å‘ç”Ÿæ”¹å˜ï¼ˆå˜ä¸º ```fulfilled``` æˆ– ```rejected``` ï¼‰ï¼Œ p çš„çŠ¶æ€å°±è·Ÿç€æ”¹å˜ã€‚å¹¶æŠŠç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªæ”¹å˜çŠ¶æ€çš„ ```promise``` çš„è¿”å›å€¼ï¼Œä¼ ç»™pçš„å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°ã€‚

            ```javascript
            // æ‰§è¡Œresolve
            var p1 = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) { 
                setTimeout(reject, 500, "one"); 
            });
            var p2 = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) { 
                setTimeout(resolve, 100, "two"); 
            });

            Promise.race([p1, p2]).then(function(value) {
                console.log('resolve', value); 
            }, function(error) {
                //not called
                console.log('reject', error); 
            });
            // è¾“å‡º
            // resolve two

            // æ‰§è¡Œreject
            var p3 = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) { 
                setTimeout(resolve, 500, "three");
            });
            var p4 = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) { 
                setTimeout(reject, 100, "four"); 
            });

            Promise.race([p3, p4]).then(function(value) {
                //not called
                console.log('resolve', value);              
            }, function(error) {
                console.log('reject', error); 
            });
            // è¾“å‡º
            // reject four
            ```
        5. ```.resolve()``` - ç«‹å³æ‰§è¡Œ ```Promise-resolve```
            > è¯­æ³•ï¼š 
            > 1. ```Promise.resolve(value);``` 
            > 2. ```Promise.resolve(promise);``` 
            > 3. ```Promise.resolve(thenable);```
            - å¯ä»¥çœ‹åš ```new Promise()``` çš„å¿«æ·æ–¹å¼

            ```javascript
            new Promise(function (resolve) {
                resolve('Success');
            });
            // ç­‰åŒäº
            Promise.resolve('Success');
            ```
